  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>I've seen the following failure when running the largedata suite:</p> 
                  <p>(emb)largedata.Derby5624Test.testDERBY_5624 used 518403 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_01_Blob used 2422 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_02_BlobNegative used 31 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_03_Clob1 used 2375 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_04_Clob2 used 3234 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_05_ClobNegative used 516 ms .<br> (net)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_01_Blob used 5360 ms .<br> (net)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_02_BlobNegative used 32 ms .<br> (net)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_03_Clob1 used 2078 ms .<br> (net)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_04_Clob2 used 2390 ms .<br> (net)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_05_ClobNegative used 938 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_01_Blob used 9188238 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_02_BlobNegative used 109 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_03_Clob1 used 8116714 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_04_Clob2 used 2164002 ms .<br> (emb)largedata.LobLimitsTest.test_05_ClobNegative used 685745 ms E<br> Time: 22,320.138<br> There was 1 error:<br> 1) LobLimitsTestjava.sql.SQLException: Table/View 'BLOBTBL' already exists in Schema 'APP'.<br> at org.apache.derby.client.am.SQLExceptionFactory40.getSQLException(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.am.SqlException.getSQLException(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.am.Statement.execute(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derbyTesting.functionTests.tests.largedata.LobLimitsTest.setupTables(LobLimitsTest.java:107)<br> at org.apache.derbyTesting.functionTests.tests.largedata.LobLimitsTest$1.decorateSQL(LobLimitsTest.java:141)<br> at org.apache.derbyTesting.junit.CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp(CleanDatabaseTestSetup.java:112)<br> at junit.extensions.TestSetup$1.protect(TestSetup.java:20)<br> at junit.extensions.TestSetup.run(TestSetup.java:25)<br> at org.apache.derbyTesting.junit.BaseTestSetup.run(BaseTestSetup.java:57)<br> at junit.extensions.TestDecorator.basicRun(TestDecorator.java:24)<br> at junit.extensions.TestSetup$1.protect(TestSetup.java:21)<br> at junit.extensions.TestSetup.run(TestSetup.java:25)<br> at junit.extensions.TestDecorator.basicRun(TestDecorator.java:24)<br> at junit.extensions.TestSetup$1.protect(TestSetup.java:21)<br> at junit.extensions.TestSetup.run(TestSetup.java:25)<br> at org.apache.derbyTesting.junit.BaseTestSetup.run(BaseTestSetup.java:57)<br> at junit.extensions.TestDecorator.basicRun(TestDecorator.java:24)<br> at junit.extensions.TestSetup$1.protect(TestSetup.java:21)<br> at junit.extensions.TestSetup.run(TestSetup.java:25)<br> Caused by: org.apache.derby.client.am.SqlException: Table/View 'BLOBTBL' already exists in Schema 'APP'.<br> at org.apache.derby.client.am.Statement.completeSqlca(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.am.Statement.completeExecuteImmediate(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.net.NetStatementReply.parseEXCSQLIMMreply(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.net.NetStatementReply.readExecuteImmediate(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.net.StatementReply.readExecuteImmediate(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.net.NetStatement.readExecuteImmediate_(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.am.Statement.readExecuteImmediate(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.am.Statement.flowExecute(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.client.am.Statement.executeX(Unknown Source)<br> ... 26 more</p> 
                  <p>Unfortunately, when this happens, there seems to be no 'fail' directory created. The derby.log in the system directory looks very innocent (just some start up and shutting down of the database), and the serverConsoleOutput.log only has the typical 'failed to find db 'wombat' messages'.</p> 
                  <p>Note, when this happens, the suite exits, so that instead of the expected 20 (or 21 on windows, see <a href="https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/DERBY-5624" title="System can run out of stack space while processing DropOnCommit requests." class="issue-link" data-issue-key="DERBY-5624"><del>DERBY-5624</del></a> for reason for skipping on Linux default installs with 1024 max open files) we only get 15 (or 16) tests run - if the test doesn't fail it goes on to run the last 5 fixtures again for network server.</p> 
                 </div> 
                </div>

Satoor\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13225626_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'08\\/Mar\\/12 22:45\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2012-03-08T22:45:55+0000\'\u003e08\\/Mar\\/12 22:45\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eThe derby.log for the passed and failed runs will show that they both have lock time outs while trying to drop the tables to get the database ready in a clean state again. The failed version has more lock time outs than the passing version. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eIt appears that CleanDatabaseTestSetup tries 5 times to drop database objects. For both passed and failed versions, all those 5 attempts fail with lock time outs. Then for some reason, in both failed and passed version, it appears that we try to drop the objects in network server mode(this is what I see in derby.log for both runs. I haven\'t looked for where it actually happens in the junit code). Both passing and failing derby.log show lock time out for drop table through network server mode. But after this failure, the passing derby.log continues to finish the large data suite with no problem. But with fail version, we get 2 more lock timeouts for trying to drop the table in network server mode. after those lock time outs, we get table already exists error in case of failing derby.log\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eSome background info on largedata._Suite\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nlargedata._Suite runs following suits\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nDerby5624Test(only f windows platform)\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nLobLimitsLiteTest\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nLobLimitsTest\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nLobLimitsClientTest\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe intermittent problem we are seeing happens while running LobLimitsTest suite. LobLimitsTest has 5 test fixtures which get run in specific order(order is ensured through TestConfiguration.orderedSuite). The intermittent problem is in the last of those 5 fixtures, namely test_05_ClobNegative. As the name indicates, this test does a bunch of negative tests but it does not do a rollback or commit at the end. test_02_BlobNegative() is the 2nd of the 5 test fixtures run by LobLimitsTest and it does negative testing too but at the end, in the catch block for the expected exception, it does a commit. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI think we may be seeing lock time outs because the transaction started by test_05_ClobNegative was never committed\\/rolled back and hence the locks were never released. I am going to make just one line change in my codeline to LobLimitsTest and add rollback() to the end of test_05_ClobNegative. I will run largedata test on my machine with that change to see how it goes. I will attach that one line change patch for reference to this jira.\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"mamtas\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13225626_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=mamtas\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"mamtas\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Mamta A. I haven\'t looked for where it actually happens in the junit code). Both passing and failing derby.log show lock time out for drop table through network server mode. But after this failure, the passing derby.log continues to finish the large data suite with no problem. But with fail version, we get 2 more lock timeouts for trying to drop the table in network server mode. after those lock time outs, we get table already exists error in case of failing derby.log \\n\\n Some background info on largedata._Suite \\nlargedata._Suite runs following suits \\nDerby5624Test(only f windows platform) \\nLobLimitsLiteTest \\nLobLimitsTest \\nLobLimitsClientTest \\n\\n The intermittent problem we are seeing happens while running LobLimitsTest suite. LobLimitsTest has 5 test fixtures which get run in specific order(order is ensured through TestConfiguration.orderedSuite). The intermittent problem is in the last of those 5 fixtures, namely test_05_ClobNegative. As the name indicates, this test does a bunch of negative tests but it does not do a rollback or commit at the end. test_02_BlobNegative() is the 2nd of the 5 test fixtures run by LobLimitsTest and it does negative testing too but at the end, in the catch block for the expected exception, it does a commit.  \\n\\n I think we may be seeing lock time outs because the transaction started by test_05_ClobNegative was never committed\\/rolled back and hence the locks were never released. I am going to make just one line change in my codeline to LobLimitsTest and add rollback() to the end of test_05_ClobNegative. I will run largedata test on my machine with that change to see how it goes. I will attach that one line change patch for reference to this jira.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-13226174\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/DERBY-5638?focusedCommentId=13226174&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-13226174\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"mamtas\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13226174_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=mamtas\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"mamtas\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Mamta A. Satoor\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13228473_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'13\\/Mar\\/12 16:02\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2012-03-13T16:02:08+0000\'\u003e13\\/Mar\\/12 16:02\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eI debugged more to see why we get 5 lock timeouts with embedded driver and then 3 locks with netwrok server before running into intermittent failure. My initial thought was that we will get 5 lock time outs both with embedded and network server before we give up trying to drop the tables.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eHere is the general flow chart from dropping tables point of view when the suite is using CleanDatabaseTestSetup. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eAt the end of the last test fixture in the suite, CleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown gets called which does following(focusing on drop table related code, ignoring the code related to dropping aliases, views etc)\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nCleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown-&gt;\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nCleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase-&gt;\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nCleanDatabaseTestSetup.removeObjects-&gt;\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\tJDBC.dropSchema-&gt;\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\t....\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\t\\/\\/ Tables\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\trs = dmd.getTables((String) null, schema, (String) null,\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n                GET_TABLES_TABLE);\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e\\tdropUsingDMD(s, rs, schema, \\\"TABLE_NAME\\\", \\\"TABLE\\\");\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\t\\t....\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\t\\/\\/ At this point there may be tables left due to\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n        \\t\\/\\/ foreign key constraints leading to a dependency loop.\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\t\\/\\/ Drop any constraints that remain and then drop the tables.\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\t\\/\\/ If there are no tables then this should be a quick no-op.\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\t.....\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\t\\/\\/ Tables (again)\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n        \\trs = dmd.getTables((String) null, schema, (String) null,\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n                \\tGET_TABLES_TABLE);        \u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\tdropUsingDMD(s, rs, schema, \\\"TABLE_NAME\\\", \\\"TABLE\\\");\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe code in dropUsingDMD is as follows\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nFirst try to drop the objects in a batch rather than individually.If there is any BatchUpdateException while dropping the objects as a batch, drop the remaining objects inidividually in a for loop. If the for loop gets\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nan exception but some of the objects before the exception got dropped successfully, then go back into the for loop and try to drop remaining objects again. This continues until either\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\na)All objects are dropped and we can return\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nb)no objects can be dropped because of exception\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eAfter this CleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown is finished(with or without success), the control goes to the CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp for the next suite. Among other things, CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp does following 2 main steps \u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n1)call CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase (drop any objects in the db)\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n2)call decorateSQL(create new objects in the db)\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eNow, let\'s go through this code in our intermittent failure case. The last test from the embedded suite LobLimitsTest finishes with no errors and we go to CleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown(). This eventually leads to JDBC.dropUsingDMD as shown above. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eIn JDBC.dropUsingDMD(), we first try to drop all the tables as a batch rather than individual drops. Here, we get the first lock timeout. Since we failed here, next we go in a loop to drop the tables individually. Here we manage to drop \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL2\\\" but get lock time out(2nd one) for trying to drop \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\". But since the loop was able to drop at least one table, we go back into the loop to try to drop remaining tables. But that results into 3rd lock timeout for \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\".  After these tries, the control goes back to JDBC.dropSchema where we try to drop the tables yet again after dropping any constraints which may be preventing the table drops(in our case, I don\'t believe we have any constraints in the db). This 2nd attempt at dropping the table takes us back to JDBC.dropUsingDMD.Again we try to drop all the tables as batch but get the 4th lock timeout for \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\". Next, we try to drop the tables inidividually in a loop, but the drop of \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\" fails with 5th lock timeout. And since we were not able to drop any table in the loop, we exit out of the loop and eventually exit out of CleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown without reporting all this as a failure even though we were not able to clean the database of it\'s objects.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eNext, before the beginning of the next suite(which in our case happens to be network server suite), we go through the CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp code. As explained earlier, one of the things that CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp does is to call CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase. Which again goes through the drop table logic as explained above. It will attempt to drop the existing tables \u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nin batch but that runs into 1st lock timeout for \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\". Next, it tries to drop the table individually, and it runs into 2nd lock timeout. Then the control goes back to CleanDatabaseTestSetup.removeObjects which calls drop table again after it drops the constraints. This time around, the batch exception runs into 3rd lock timeout exception. With my understanding of\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nthe code, we should have run into 4th lock timeout trying to drop the table individually but for some reason, I don\'t see that 4th lock time out with DRDA driver in derby.log. In any case, we once again exit \u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nCleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase without successfully getting rid of all the tables and next step in CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp is the call to decorateSQL().decorateSQL fails when it tries to create tables but they already exist in the database becaue CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase was not able to get rid of them and that is why we get the exception Table\\/View \'BLOBTBL\' already exists in Schema \'APP\'.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI am not sure why this locking issue is only intermittent but atleast we understand what is happening during the suite runs.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eNot sure if it is correct for CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase to run into exceptions while doing the cleanup but ignore those exceptions. I ran into a very old jira \u003ca href=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/browse\\/DERBY-2220\\\" title=\\\"Uncommitted transactions executed throught XAResource will held locks after the application terminates (or crashes during the transaction).\\\" class=\\\"issue-link\\\" data-issue-key=\\\"DERBY-2220\\\"\u003e\u003cdel\u003eDERBY-2220\u003c\\/del\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e(Uncommitted transactions executed throught XAResource will held locks after the application terminates (or crashes during the transaction).) where there was a brief conversation about how may be CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase should drop the database if it is not able to drop the objects inside the database. Here is part of Dan Debrunner\'s comment on that issue\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n******************\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nI also think that you\'ve found an issue in the clean database decorator and as \u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nsuch it would be good to fix it centrally there, rather than in a single test. \u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nfor example, if the clean database decorator failed to cleanup the database, \u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nit could report the failure and then blow away the database.\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n******************\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eWe can do atleast one of the two things for this particular jira at this point (or may be even both)\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n1)Have CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase report that it is having trouble deleting the objects and hence it will drop the database and create the objects mentioned in decorateSQL. This will get rid of intermittent failures in large data suite but it will not explain why do we intermittently run into lock timeouts\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n2)Debug why we are running into intermittently lock timeouts with large data suite. I am running the tests with derby.locks.deadlockTrace=true to see if it will give us more information about the locks.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ePlease let me know if there are any other options we could be pursuing.\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"mamtas\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13228473_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=mamtas\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"mamtas\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Mamta A. Satoor\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13228473_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'13\\/Mar\\/12 16:02\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2012-03-13T16:02:08+0000\'\u003e13\\/Mar\\/12 16:02\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    I debugged more to see why we get 5 lock timeouts with embedded driver and then 3 locks with netwrok server before running into intermittent failure. My initial thought was that we will get 5 lock time outs both with embedded and network server before we give up trying to drop the tables. \\n\\n Here is the general flow chart from dropping tables point of view when the suite is using CleanDatabaseTestSetup.  \\n\\n At the end of the last test fixture in the suite, CleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown gets called which does following(focusing on drop table related code, ignoring the code related to dropping aliases, views etc) \\nCleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown-&gt; \\nCleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase-&gt; \\nCleanDatabaseTestSetup.removeObjects-&gt; \\n\\tJDBC.dropSchema-&gt; \\n\\t.... \\n\\t\\/\\/ Tables \\n\\trs = dmd.getTables((String) null, schema, (String) null, \\n                GET_TABLES_TABLE); \\n\\n \\tdropUsingDMD(s, rs, schema, \\\"TABLE_NAME\\\", \\\"TABLE\\\"); \\n\\t\\t.... \\n\\t\\/\\/ At this point there may be tables left due to \\n        \\t\\/\\/ foreign key constraints leading to a dependency loop. \\n\\t\\/\\/ Drop any constraints that remain and then drop the tables. \\n\\t\\/\\/ If there are no tables then this should be a quick no-op. \\n\\t..... \\n\\t\\/\\/ Tables (again) \\n        \\trs = dmd.getTables((String) null, schema, (String) null, \\n                \\tGET_TABLES_TABLE);         \\n\\tdropUsingDMD(s, rs, schema, \\\"TABLE_NAME\\\", \\\"TABLE\\\"); \\n\\n The code in dropUsingDMD is as follows \\nFirst try to drop the objects in a batch rather than individually.If there is any BatchUpdateException while dropping the objects as a batch, drop the remaining objects inidividually in a for loop. If the for loop gets \\nan exception but some of the objects before the exception got dropped successfully, then go back into the for loop and try to drop remaining objects again. This continues until either \\na)All objects are dropped and we can return \\nb)no objects can be dropped because of exception \\n\\n After this CleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown is finished(with or without success), the control goes to the CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp for the next suite. Among other things, CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp does following 2 main steps  \\n1)call CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase (drop any objects in the db) \\n2)call decorateSQL(create new objects in the db) \\n\\n Now, let\'s go through this code in our intermittent failure case. The last test from the embedded suite LobLimitsTest finishes with no errors and we go to CleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown(). This eventually leads to JDBC.dropUsingDMD as shown above.  \\n\\n In JDBC.dropUsingDMD(), we first try to drop all the tables as a batch rather than individual drops. Here, we get the first lock timeout. Since we failed here, next we go in a loop to drop the tables individually. Here we manage to drop \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL2\\\" but get lock time out(2nd one) for trying to drop \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\". But since the loop was able to drop at least one table, we go back into the loop to try to drop remaining tables. But that results into 3rd lock timeout for \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\".  After these tries, the control goes back to JDBC.dropSchema where we try to drop the tables yet again after dropping any constraints which may be preventing the table drops(in our case, I don\'t believe we have any constraints in the db). This 2nd attempt at dropping the table takes us back to JDBC.dropUsingDMD.Again we try to drop all the tables as batch but get the 4th lock timeout for \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\". Next, we try to drop the tables inidividually in a loop, but the drop of \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\" fails with 5th lock timeout. And since we were not able to drop any table in the loop, we exit out of the loop and eventually exit out of CleanDatabaseTestSetup.tearDown without reporting all this as a failure even though we were not able to clean the database of it\'s objects. \\n\\n Next, before the beginning of the next suite(which in our case happens to be network server suite), we go through the CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp code. As explained earlier, one of the things that CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp does is to call CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase. Which again goes through the drop table logic as explained above. It will attempt to drop the existing tables  \\nin batch but that runs into 1st lock timeout for \\\"APP\\\".\\\"CLOBTBL\\\". Next, it tries to drop the table individually, and it runs into 2nd lock timeout. Then the control goes back to CleanDatabaseTestSetup.removeObjects which calls drop table again after it drops the constraints. This time around, the batch exception runs into 3rd lock timeout exception. With my understanding of \\nthe code, we should have run into 4th lock timeout trying to drop the table individually but for some reason, I don\'t see that 4th lock time out with DRDA driver in derby.log. In any case, we once again exit  \\nCleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase without successfully getting rid of all the tables and next step in CleanDatabaseTestSetup.setUp is the call to decorateSQL().decorateSQL fails when it tries to create tables but they already exist in the database becaue CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase was not able to get rid of them and that is why we get the exception Table\\/View \'BLOBTBL\' already exists in Schema \'APP\'. \\n\\n I am not sure why this locking issue is only intermittent but atleast we understand what is happening during the suite runs. \\n\\n Not sure if it is correct for CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase to run into exceptions while doing the cleanup but ignore those exceptions. I ran into a very old jira   DERBY-2220  (Uncommitted transactions executed throught XAResource will held locks after the application terminates (or crashes during the transaction).) where there was a brief conversation about how may be CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase should drop the database if it is not able to drop the objects inside the database. Here is part of Dan Debrunner\'s comment on that issue \\n****************** \\nI also think that you\'ve found an issue in the clean database decorator and as  \\nsuch it would be good to fix it centrally there, rather than in a single test.  \\nfor example, if the clean database decorator failed to cleanup the database,  \\nit could report the failure and then blow away the database. \\n****************** \\n\\n We can do atleast one of the two things for this particular jira at this point (or may be even both) \\n1)Have CleanDatabaseTestSetup.cleanDatabase report that it is having trouble deleting the objects and hence it will drop the database and create the objects mentioned in decorateSQL. This will get rid of intermittent failures in large data suite but it will not explain why do we intermittently run into lock timeouts \\n2)Debug why we are running into intermittently lock timeouts with large data suite. I am running the tests with derby.locks.deadlockTrace=true to see if it will give us more information about the locks. \\n\\n Please let me know if there are any other options we could be pursuing. \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13229992_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'15\\/Mar\\/12 08:54\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2012-03-15T08:54:44+0000\'\u003e15\\/Mar\\/12 08:54\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eIf there\'s an index on the table whose rows are deleted, there will be post-commit work scheduled that could hold locks when tearDown() is executed. If that\'s what\'s causing the timeouts, you might try one of these approaches:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e1) Wait for post-commit to finish after having deleted the rows. This can be done by calling T_Access.waitForPostCommitToFinish() in a stored procedure after deleteTable(). See ReleaseCompileLocksTest for an example.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e2) Use TRUNCATE TABLE instead of DELETE in the deleteTable() method. In addition to being faster on large tables, it also avoids post-commit work and shouldn\'t cause any concurrent locking to happen during tearDown().\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"knutanders\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13229992_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=knutanders\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"knutanders\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Knut Anders Hatlen\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13229992_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'15\\/Mar\\/12 08:54\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2012-03-15T08:54:44+0000\'\u003e15\\/Mar\\/12 08:54\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    If there\'s an index on the table whose rows are deleted, there will be post-commit work scheduled that could hold locks when tearDown() is executed. If that\'s what\'s causing the timeouts, you might try one of these approaches: \\n\\n 1) Wait for post-commit to finish after having deleted the rows. This can be done by calling T_Access.waitForPostCommitToFinish() in a stored procedure after deleteTable(). See ReleaseCompileLocksTest for an example. \\n\\n 2) Use TRUNCATE TABLE instead of DELETE in the deleteTable() method. In addition to being faster on large tables, it also avoids post-commit work and shouldn\'t cause any concurrent locking to happen during tearDown().              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-13230335\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/DERBY-5638?focusedCommentId=13230335&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-13230335\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"mamtas\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13230335_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=mamtas\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"mamtas\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Mamta A. Satoor\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13230335_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'15\\/Mar\\/12 17:25\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2012-03-15T17:25:11+0000\'\u003e15\\/Mar\\/12 17:25\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eHi Knut, I appreciate you taking the time to look at this. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI have another alternative approach(which requires just one line change to large data suite network server run) to fix the problem with intermittent lock time out issues possibly because of background threads trying to finish post-commit changes related to large objects. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe issue has been that the CleanDatabaseTestSetup , after the last test fixture of embedded suite is done, tries to drop the tables but runs into lock timeout errors and hence it never finishes dropping the tables. None of these errors get reported anywhere by CleanDatabaseTestSetup and we simply move on to the next suite which in our case is network server running the large data tests. As part of CleanDatabaseTestSetup decorator for network server, we try to drop the existing objects in the database again before creating the new objects required by the new suite and the drop tables again run into lock timeouts. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eWhat I am suggesting as a solution is to have the network server suite use a brand new database to do it\'s testing via singleUseDatabaseDecorator and that way it will not run into locks held on the database used by the embedded run of large data tests. The change is fairly easy(just one line change) in LobLimitsClientTest.suite(). The changed LobLimitsClientTest,suite looks as follows\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n    public static Test suite() \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n{\\n        return TestConfiguration.singleUseDatabaseDecorator(\\n             TestConfiguration.clientServerDecorator(LobLimitsTest.suite()));\\n    }\\n\u003cp\u003eThe original LobLimitsClientTest,suite() in svn looks as follows\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n     public static Test suite() \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n{\\n        return TestConfiguration.clientServerDecorator(LobLimitsTest.suite());\\n     }\\n\u003cp\u003e }\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI ran the large data suite twice on my machine with this change and I don\'t see the lock timeout from network server in the log file anymore. I will go ahead and commit this change.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eAdditionally, I will create a new jira for CleanDatabaseTestSetup about not reporting failures while trying to clean the database by dropping the objects., Either, it should report those errors in fail directory or somewhere else so we can diagnose more easily if the subsequent suite fails because of left over database objects from the previous suite. Or it can try to drop the objects as it does but if it can\'t drop them successfully, then it should drop the database and create a brand new database which is clean for the next suite to use. One of the things that CleanDatabaseTestSetup can do is what Knut suggested. Do TRUNCATE TABLE if it is having trouble dropping the tables and then try to drop the tables again or wait for post-commit to finish by calling T_Access.waitForPostCommitToFinish() before dropping objects from the database.\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"mamtas\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13230335_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=mamtas\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"mamtas\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Mamta A. Satoor\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13230335_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'15\\/Mar\\/12 17:25\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2012-03-15T17:25:11+0000\'\u003e15\\/Mar\\/12 17:25\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    Hi Knut, I appreciate you taking the time to look at this.  \\n\\n I have another alternative approach(which requires just one line change to large data suite network server run) to fix the problem with intermittent lock time out issues possibly because of background threads trying to finish post-commit changes related to large objects.  \\n\\n The issue has been that the CleanDatabaseTestSetup , after the last test fixture of embedded suite is done, tries to drop the tables but runs into lock timeout errors and hence it never finishes dropping the tables. None of these errors get reported anywhere by CleanDatabaseTestSetup and we simply move on to the next suite which in our case is network server running the large data tests. As part of CleanDatabaseTestSetup decorator for network server, we try to drop the existing objects in the database again before creating the new objects required by the new suite and the drop tables again run into lock timeouts.  \\n\\n What I am suggesting as a solution is to have the network server suite use a brand new database to do it\'s testing via singleUseDatabaseDecorator and that way it will not run into locks held on the database used by the embedded run of large data tests. The change is fairly easy(just one line change) in LobLimitsClientTest.suite(). The changed LobLimitsClientTest,suite looks as follows \\n    public static Test suite()  \\n{\\n        return TestConfiguration.singleUseDatabaseDecorator(\\n             TestConfiguration.clientServerDecorator(LobLimitsTest.suite()));\\n    }\\n The original LobLimitsClientTest,suite() in svn looks as follows \\n     public static Test suite()  \\n{\\n        return TestConfiguration.clientServerDecorator(LobLimitsTest.suite());\\n     }\\n  } \\n\\n\\n I ran the large data suite twice on my machine with this change and I don\'t see the lock timeout from network server in the log file anymore. I will go ahead and commit this change. \\n\\n Additionally, I will create a new jira for CleanDatabaseTestSetup about not reporting failures while trying to clean the database by dropping the objects., Either, it should report those errors in fail directory or somewhere else so we can diagnose more easily if the subsequent suite fails because of left over database objects from the previous suite. Or it can try to drop the objects as it does but if it can\'t drop them successfully, then it should drop the database and create a brand new database which is clean for the next suite to use. One of the things that CleanDatabaseTestSetup can do is what Knut suggested. Do TRUNCATE TABLE if it is having trouble dropping the tables and then try to drop the tables again or wait for post-commit to finish by calling T_Access.waitForPostCommitToFinish() before dropping objects from the database.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv and he mentioned that if we actually look at the number in the log file names(for eg for428.dat), we will see that Derby didn\'t have to write as much to the log when we use truncate table which is a good sign. As can be seen above, with truncate table, the last log files name is log428.dat whereas log file name with trunk codeline run is log441.dat  \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe reason we see large number of log files with truncate table is that probably a checkpoint was not issued. Checkpoints are issued periodically and among other things, it;s frequency also depends on how many log files have been written so far.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI tried connecting to the wombat directory with large number of log files through ij and after getting out of ij, I saw that there were only 3 log files left in log directory as shown below\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n$ ls -l\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\ntotal 1026\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n----------+ 1 mamta mkgroup      48 Mar 20 10:20 log.ctrl\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n----------+ 1 mamta mkgroup 1048576 Mar 20 10:20 log428.dat\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n----------+ 1 mamta mkgroup      48 Mar 20 10:20 logmirror.ctrl\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe reason for reduction in number of log files is as part of booting up wombat through ij, we applied all the left over log files to the database and hence as part of recovery, the log files were deleted since they are not needed any more.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eBased on this experiment, in addition to having truncate table in deleteTable() method, I plan on adding a test fixture to LobLimitsTest class and that test fixture will just shutodwn the databases. As part of the shutdown, the logs will get applied and hence at the end of the suite, the size of the wombat database will be much smaller and there won\'t be left over huge log files left behind after a successful run.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eOnce I have the tests running successfully with this change and verify that log directory is indeed much smaller, i will post a patch.\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"mamtas\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13233931_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=mamtas\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"mamtas\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Mamta A.
